padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1264621">Fragrant Lily</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-02">03/02/24 17:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I fell in love with this fragrance from the first sniff. Probably I've been charmed so much by its name that my imagination drew a picture of the sweet sirens' voices carrying enchanted sailors towards dangerous rocks straight away. The rose I smell here is caught by the marine notes and aroma of algae. This gives a bewitching feeling of a revived ancient legend, in which the earthy is mixed with the fabulous. The boozy twist of the scent gives more colours to the whole story and makes it vivid, almost real: the sweet vanilla song of the sea beauties is putting half-drunk and half-sober sailors into a trance. Leather and patchouli undertones hint at the tragic ends of the story, beautiful and dramatic of the same time. I absolutely love this fragrance!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53042"comment_id="2080366"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jusbox/Siren-Sailors-53042.html?ccid=2080366#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2023715" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1322784">InfiniteStarla</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-09">11/09/23 08:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I smelt a few in the range in store, and liked this one and Cheeky Smile on first impression. Luckily managed to get a branded sample from the Selfridges counter which was great. On first wearing today, it's been really enjoyable. The initial blast is a bit rough; although there is a floral sweetness that lends a typically girly/flirty vibe, there is also more than just a hint of something dark and troubled, in the form of those boozy notes. Initially I find it a bit unbalanced, like a bitterness lurking, but after the first 10 minutes or so this settles down. In the dry down and throughout the wear I get a fruity, slightly tart rosiness. It's kind of syrupy in vibe, not too thick or heavy, but almost like Calpol with it's palpable granulated sugary pinkness.  It doesn't become too sweet on me though either, and the longevity and sillage are excellent - I'm getting wafts still after 8 hours.  I don't think it's ultimately "me", but I thoroughly enjoyed wearing it and found it to surpass my expectations. I smelt Roses Vanille a long time ago, but remember that to be spicy / have obvious Middle Eastern leanings - I don't detect that here at all, so wouldn't say they're similar at all (it's been a good year or two since smelling RV though so perhaps my memory isn't good).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1278843">Devilish Scents</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-29">09/29/23 15:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This may be more femme to some, but I absolutely love the scent. The fruity rose opening is pretty loud that softens to a cloud on the skin. I would say the fruity rose lasts through the mid that seamlessly enhances with a boozy rum/Cognac accord that makes it naughty/sexy. The mid point makes it a bit more unisex in my opinion with the boozy accords. Although fruity, the boozy accords make it more dirty and inherently masculine in my eyes. The dry down still retains a floral sweetness but turned down, and mostly taken over by a vanilla musky cloud of sex. I believe the suede is just adding a bit of of that sexy touch that I find so seductive such as Amy Winehouse's smoky voice/demeanor. I believe this may be a bit overpriced but it lasts all day on skin with many provocative transitions on the skin to make it more interesting. The presentation has a nice aesthetic and I feel this scent is a perfect representation of Amy Winehouse soul/seductive music with a touch of sexy/dirty glamour. Overall a sexy scent, great for Spring and fall. but could be pulled off any time of year. I feel this is a type of scent that will smell different on each persons skin depending on chemistry and will overall smell different depending on season as well. <br />
RIP AMY WINEHOUSE, I loved your music and you will be missed.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53042"comment_id="1940531"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jusbox/Siren-Sailors-53042.html?ccid=1940531#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1923299" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1269760" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SailorV"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/955817"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.955817.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SailorV" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1269760ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1269760" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/955817">SailorV</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-01-03">01/03/21 05:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After I read the rather unimpressed reviews for this fragrance, I was positively surprised by how good it smells. Guess I'm lucky to perceive it quite differently from the other reviewers!<br />
I generally don't like to put fragrances into specific age groups, but if I try to think of a typical teen scent or fragrances marketed to children, this is really not what comes to my mind. Not at all. Neither do I smell huge similarities to Mancera Roses Vanilla. <br />
I would categorize Siren &amp; Sailors roughly into the same group as many intense/elixir/night versions of feminine designer perfumes, which is a good thing to me. <br />
<br />
The loudest notes are juicy peaches and bright pink roses drenched in syrup, but there's more to it. I really get the boozy whiskey and rum notes in the opening and the suede in the base. They give the fragrance substance while also being softened by the rose and peach, a dark vanilla, a little patchouli and balsamic notes.<br />
This is a sweet and feminine fragrance, but with some spiciness and warmth. Cozy and sexy at once. It makes me think of a sunset color scheme of pinks, red and oranges.<br />
<br />
I think this deserves more praise and I would recommend it to anyone who likes gourmandish roses.<br />
It might not be groundbreaking, but very, very well-done, smoothly blended and with a nice twist to it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53042"comment_id="1269760"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jusbox/Siren-Sailors-53042.html?ccid=1269760#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1239456" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1269760" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="SailorV"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/955817"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.955817.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="SailorV" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1269760ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1269760" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/955817">SailorV</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-01-03">01/03/21 05:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After I read the rather unimpressed reviews for this fragrance, I was positively surprised by how good it smells. Guess I'm lucky to perceive it quite differently from the other reviewers!<br />
I generally don't like to put fragrances into specific age groups, but if I try to think of a typical teen scent or fragrances marketed to children, this is really not what comes to my mind. Not at all. Neither do I smell huge similarities to Mancera Roses Vanilla. <br />
I would categorize Siren &amp; Sailors roughly into the same group as many intense/elixir/night versions of feminine designer perfumes, which is a good thing to me. <br />
<br />
The loudest notes are juicy peaches and bright pink roses drenched in syrup, but there's more to it. I really get the boozy whiskey and rum notes in the opening and the suede in the base. They give the fragrance substance while also being softened by the rose and peach, a dark vanilla, a little patchouli and balsamic notes.<br />
This is a sweet and feminine fragrance, but with some spiciness and warmth. Cozy and sexy at once. It makes me think of a sunset color scheme of pinks, red and oranges.<br />
<br />
I think this deserves more praise and I would recommend it to anyone who likes gourmandish roses.<br />
It might not be groundbreaking, but very, very well-done, smoothly blended and with a nice twist to it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53042"comment_id="1269760"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jusbox/Siren-Sailors-53042.html?ccid=1269760#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1846303" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The Dior is as expected, classy, timeless, softly and sweetly rosey, speaking of the chypre decades, beautiful. But this Sirens and Sailors is blowing my socks off. Opens with a white sugar bubblegummy peony-ish rose quickly joined by a boozy and slightly leathery darkness. The cristalline feel persists. Beautiful throw. I can see the comparisons with Roses Vanille which has a similar white sugar rose but goes in a more herbal slightly spiced direction plus a more oriental vanilla base. I‚Äôve been on a sampling binge craving something ‚Äòdifferent‚Äô. This happens to me every couple of years üôÑ. I‚Äôve been through 10ml of Baccarat R trying to see the magic in it and failing. Suddenly, Magic has arrived.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53042"comment_id="1846303"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jusbox/Siren-Sailors-53042.html?ccid=1846303#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1792801" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I get loads of rose, rum and vanilla, with a bit of suede and musk in the dry-down. Apparently this is inspired by Amy Winehouse and I think that‚Äôs spot on - it‚Äôs got an old-school femininity from the rose, but then a dark, dirty edge from the booze. It‚Äôs sweet but I wouldn‚Äôt say young; maybe suits a woman in their 20s or 30s. Best for nighttime.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="53042"comment_id="1792801"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Jusbox/Siren-Sailors-53042.html?ccid=1792801#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1969390" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; About her hypnotic voice, a gift from her, her sweet and tormented personality, which will mark her throughout her short life.<br />

A fragrance that I really like and ended up on my wishlist, truly wonderful, beautiful and delicate like a rose, but surrounded by thorns.<br />
I want to quote the words of one of the most beautiful songs in my opinion by this artist, "Stronger than me", with a heart full of gratitude for having given us, even if for a short time, the beauty of her voice and her music.<br />
